</ul></nav><div class="bricks-mobile-menu-overlay"></div></div><div data-script-id="binpne" class="brxe-code member-icon"><div class="member-avatar account-button" id="userAvatar" data-gtm-event="firebaseLoginInit"> <div class="anonymous-avatar"></div><div class="status-indicator">&times;</div></div></div></div></div></header><main id="brx-content"><section id="brxe-gftejx" class="brxe-section drifted-slider"><script>document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function (){
const wrappers=document.querySelectorAll(".drifted-slider-wrapper");
wrappers.forEach((wrapper)=> {
const track=wrapper.querySelector(".drifted-slider-track");
const prevBtn=wrapper.querySelector(".drifted-prev");
const nextBtn=wrapper.querySelector(".drifted-next");
function updateButtons(){
const scrollLeft=track.scrollLeft;
const maxScrollLeft=track.scrollWidth - track.clientWidth;
prevBtn.disabled=scrollLeft <=0;
nextBtn.disabled=scrollLeft >=maxScrollLeft - 1;
}
prevBtn.addEventListener("click", ()=> {
track.scrollBy({ left: -wrapper.offsetWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
});
nextBtn.addEventListener("click", ()=> {
track.scrollBy({ left: wrapper.offsetWidth, behavior: 'smooth' });
});
track.addEventListener("scroll", updateButtons);
window.addEventListener("resize", updateButtons);
updateButtons();
let isDown=false;
let startX;
let scrollLeft;
track.addEventListener("mousedown", (e)=> {
isDown=true;
track.classList.add("dragging");
startX=e.pageX - track.offsetLeft;
scrollLeft=track.scrollLeft;
e.preventDefault();
});
track.addEventListener("mouseleave", ()=> {
isDown=false;
track.classList.remove("dragging");
});
track.addEventListener("mouseup", ()=> {
isDown=false;
track.classList.remove("dragging");
});
let isClick=false;
track.addEventListener("mousedown", (e)=> {
isDown=true;
isClick=true;
startX=e.pageX - track.offsetLeft;
scrollLeft=track.scrollLeft;
track.classList.add("dragging");
e.preventDefault();
});
track.addEventListener("mousemove", (e)=> {
if(!isDown) return;
const x=e.pageX - track.offsetLeft;
const walk=(x - startX) * 1.5;
if(Math.abs(walk) > 5) isClick=false;
track.scrollLeft=scrollLeft - walk;
});
track.addEventListener("mouseup", (e)=> {
isDown=false;
track.classList.remove("dragging");
if(isClick){
const target=e.target.closest(".drifted-slide[data-href]");
if(target&&target.dataset.href){
window.location.href=target.dataset.href;
}}
});
track.addEventListener("mousemove", (e)=> {
if(!isDown) return;
const x=e.pageX - track.offsetLeft;
const walk=(x - startX) * 1.5;
track.scrollLeft=scrollLeft - walk;
});
const slides=wrapper.querySelectorAll(".drifted-slide");
slides.forEach((slide)=> {
const videoBg=slide.querySelector(".drifted-video-bg");
if(!videoBg) return;
const img=videoBg.querySelector("img");
slide.addEventListener("mouseenter", ()=> {
if(!videoBg.querySelector("video")){
const videoUrl=videoBg.dataset.videoUrl;
if(videoUrl){
const video=document.createElement("video");
video.src=videoUrl;
video.autoplay=true;
video.muted=true;
video.loop=true;
video.playsInline=true;
video.style.position="absolute";
video.style.top=0;
video.style.left=0;
video.style.width="100%";
video.style.height="100%";
video.style.objectFit="cover";
video.addEventListener("loadeddata", ()=> {
video.classList.add("active");
});
videoBg.appendChild(video);
if(img) img.style.opacity="0";
}}
});
slide.addEventListener("mouseleave", ()=> {
const video=videoBg.querySelector("video");
if(video) video.remove();
if(img) img.style.opacity="1";
});
});
});
});</script><div class="brxe-container drifted-slider-wrapper"><button class="brxe-button drifted-slider-btn drifted-prev bricks-button">&#10094;</button><div class="brxe-div article-card-juliet__date">Car Games,</div></div></a><div class="brxe-2cf8fc brxe-container"><div class="brxe-201607 brxe-div drifted-card-meta"><div class="brxe-jtzuyd brxe-text-basic">February 2, 2026</div><div class="brxe-wjyysn brxe-text-basic"></div></div><h3 class="brxe-00a5a2 brxe-heading drifted-card-heading"><a href="https://www.drifted.com/burnout-crazy-drift/" title="Read more about Burnout Crazy Drift" aria-label="Read more about Burnout Crazy Drift">Burnout Crazy Drift </a></h3><p class="brxe-250bd4 brxe-text-basic drifted-card-excerpt">Tandem or battle a selection of ready-to-slide, pre-tuned iconic JDM legends in this entry-level browser drifter with smooth physics.</p></div></li></ul><div class="brxe-div"><div class="brxe-inverted-pagination brx-infinite-scroll-pagination" data-query-element-id="ad6741" data-infinite="true"><div class="brx-load-more-wrapper"><a href="https://www.drifted.com/page/252/" class="brx-load-more-button">Load more</a></div></div></div></section><div data-script-id="kxngbm" class="brxe-code"><script>(function(){
var LEADERBOARD_URLS={
daily: 'https://www.drifted.com/wp-content/leaderboards/daily.json',
driftAttack: 'https://www.drifted.com/wp-content/leaderboards/drift_attack.json'
};
function generateCacheBuster(){
var now=Date.now();
var fiveMinuteInterval=5 * 60 * 1000;
return Math.floor(now / fiveMinuteInterval);
}
function formatNumber(num){
return num.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ',');
}
function createRow(rank, rankClass, name, meta, score){
var row=document.createElement('div');
row.className='dhm-leaderboard-row';
var rankDiv=document.createElement('div');
rankDiv.className='dhm-rank ' + rankClass;
rankDiv.textContent='#' + rank;
var playerInfo=document.createElement('div');
playerInfo.className='dhm-player-info';
var playerName=document.createElement('div');
playerName.className='dhm-player-name';
playerName.textContent=name;
var playerMeta=document.createElement('div');
playerMeta.className='dhm-player-meta';
playerMeta.textContent=meta;
playerInfo.appendChild(playerName);
playerInfo.appendChild(playerMeta);
var scoreDiv=document.createElement('div');
scoreDiv.className='dhm-score';
scoreDiv.textContent=score;
row.appendChild(rankDiv);
row.appendChild(playerInfo);
row.appendChild(scoreDiv);
return row;
}
function loadDailyLeaderboard(){
var container=document.querySelector('.daily-leaderboard');
if(!container) return;
var cacheBuster=generateCacheBuster();
fetch(LEADERBOARD_URLS.daily + '?v=' + cacheBuster)
.then(function(response){
if(!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed');
return response.json();
})
.then(function(data){
container.innerHTML='';
if(!data.leaderboard||data.leaderboard.length===0){
var errorDiv=document.createElement('div');
errorDiv.className='dhm-error';
errorDiv.textContent='No players yet today. Be the first!';
container.appendChild(errorDiv);
return;
}
var topPlayers=data.leaderboard.slice(0, 100);
for (var i=0; i < topPlayers.length; i++){
var player=topPlayers[i];
var rankClass=i===0 ? 'top-1':i===1 ? 'top-2':i===2 ? 'top-3':'';
var meta=player.raceCount + ' races - Avg: ' + formatNumber(Math.round(player.averageEarnings));
var score='$' + formatNumber(player.totalEarnings);
var row=createRow(player.rank, rankClass, player.displayName, meta, score);
container.appendChild(row);
}})
.catch(function(error){
console.error('Error loading daily leaderboard:', error);
container.innerHTML='';
var errorDiv=document.createElement('div');
errorDiv.className='dhm-error';
errorDiv.textContent='Failed to load leaderboard.';
container.appendChild(errorDiv);
});
}
function loadDriftAttackLeaderboard(){
var container=document.querySelector('.drift-leaderboard');
if(!container) return;
fetch(LEADERBOARD_URLS.driftAttack)
.then(function(response){
if(!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed');
return response.json();
})
.then(function(data){
container.innerHTML='';
if(!data.leaderboard||data.leaderboard.length===0){
var errorDiv=document.createElement('div');
errorDiv.className='dhm-error';
errorDiv.textContent='No drift scores yet. Start drifting!';
container.appendChild(errorDiv);
return;
}
var topPlayers=data.leaderboard.slice(0, 100);
for (var i=0; i < topPlayers.length; i++){
var player=topPlayers[i];
var rankClass=i===0 ? 'top-1':i===1 ? 'top-2':i===2 ? 'top-3':'';
var meta=player.bestTrack + ' - ' + player.bestCar;
var score=formatNumber(player.bestScore);
var row=createRow(player.rank, rankClass, player.displayName, meta, score);
container.appendChild(row);
}})
.catch(function(error){
console.error('Error loading drift attack leaderboard:', error);
container.innerHTML='';
var errorDiv=document.createElement('div');
errorDiv.className='dhm-error';
errorDiv.textContent='Failed to load leaderboard.';
container.appendChild(errorDiv);
});
}
function initLeaderboards(){
loadDailyLeaderboard();
loadDriftAttackLeaderboard();
setInterval(loadDailyLeaderboard, 5 * 60 * 1000);
}
if(document.readyState==='loading'){
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initLeaderboards);
}else{
initLeaderboards();
}})();</script></div></main><footer id="brx-footer"><div class="brxe-section perfmatters-lazy-element drifted-footer-wrapper"><div id="brxe-6bd1d1" class="brxe-container drifted-footer-block1"><div }};};

}}else{

}})
.catch(err=> {

});
});
}
